Here is Vita DAO for who wants to learn more about them! [https://www.vita-dao.io/](https://www.vita-dao.io/)

VitaDAO

VitaDAO is the world‚Äôs first decentralised intellectual property collective. Its mission is to extend the human lifespan by researching, financing, and commercialising longevity therapeutics in an open and democratic manner. VitaDAO is a web3-based decentralised autonomous organisation (DAO).

![https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/600ff0f8154936050d98ec01/60557c944e987f80023926dc_VitaDAO%20Opengraph.png](https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/600ff0f8154936050d98ec01/60557c944e987f80023926dc_VitaDAO%20Opengraph.png)

Hey @everyone for what it's worth I want to let everyone know that I asked for help on the #support channel on Origin Protocol's discord server. I've gotten TWO of these kinds of scammer solicitations in my DMs already! Stay alert. Stay safe!

Join the Token Engineering Commons!

Advancing the field of token engineering in a regenerative way. Stewarding the cultivation of resources to accelerate the creation of robustly engineered models, modular tools, standards and educational opportunities.

_16-Sep-21 10:46 AM_:

Re praise convo. One of the issues brought up is that as we scale people will have trouble quantifying accurately because people don't know what other people are doing. Actually this is one of the major second order benefits of praise, that the quantifiers get awareness about other things that other people are doing. This ties things together within the community, the quantifiers become aware of who is doing a great job in the eyes of the community.

Jain vegetarianism

Jain vegetarianism is practiced by the followers of Jain culture and philosophy. It is one of the most rigorous forms of spiritually motivated diet on the Indian subcontinent and beyond. The Jain cuisine is completely lacto vegetarian and also excludes underground vegetables such as potato, garlic, onion etc, to prevent injuring small insects an...

_08-Oct-21 11:54 AM_:

Here's the link to Roam from our call today: [https://roamresearch.com/](https://roamresearch.com/)

Roam Research ‚Äì A note taking tool for networked thought.

As easy to use as a word document or bulleted list, and as powerful for finding, collecting, and connecting related ideas as a graph database. Collaborate with others in real time, or store all your data locally.

![https://roamresearch.com/assets/astro.png](https://roamresearch.com/assets/astro.png)

Join the Token Engineering Commons!

Advancing the field of token engineering in a regenerative way. Stewarding the cultivation of resources to accelerate the creation of robustly engineered models, modular tools, standards and educational opportunities.

![https://tec-web.netlify.app/images/Share.jpg](https://tec-web.netlify.app/images/Share.jpg)

Welcome to TEC Source

TEC Source is here to provide easy access to active and archived documents within the TEC. If you are currently working on a document and want to share it here, please notify one of our Stewards!

![https://app.gitbook.com/share/space/thumbnail/-Mj5bOyMOomkgNfE--be.png?color=%23A44EED&logo=&theme=dark](https://app.gitbook.com/share/space/thumbnail/-Mj5bOyMOomkgNfE--be.png?color=%23A44EED&logo=&theme=dark)

_19-Jan-22 06:30 PM_:

re: alternatives to metaverse landowner monopolies and token models that can enable it Hi all - anyone here thinking about, or witness to an alternative paradigm on metaverse land? what i mean is there is much speculation about owning real estate in the metaverse(s) - but this is a very web2 capitalist idea! Maybe land grabs prevail, or maybe there is some new paradigm that makes spatial value more portable depending on who and what is transpiring. why should it be tied to land? It would really suck if metaverses just copy today's landowner monopolies. Hope this makes sense. Thanks for considering.

_28-Jan-22 07:37 AM_:

Hi, I wasn't sure where to post this. I've been studying your governance model a little bit, and was thinking about your token model and governance. I'm by no means anyone who has much knowledge about token engineering/economics. But I had a thought that I wondered about, of which you probably already have thought of. So, theoretically someone with a lot lot of money could very easily buy governance rights from the ABC (I guess the voter pamphlet also looks at such scenario's). And in theory quadratic token-weighted voting on snapshot would be quite susceptible to a sybil attack also, right? Is the Celeste arbitration protocol then the response that you would have to such risks?

JosephS

[Hi, I wasn't sure where to post this. I've been studying your governance model a little bit, and was thinking about your token model and governance. I'm by no means anyone who has much knowledge about token engineering/economics. But I had a thought that I wondered about, of which you probably already have thought of. So, theoretically someone with a lot lot of money could very easily buy governance rights from the ABC (I guess the voter pamphlet also looks at such scenario's). And in theory quadratic token-weighted voting on snapshot would be quite susceptible to a sybil attack also, right? Is the Celeste arbitration protocol then the response that you would have to such risks?](about:blank#)

<h3>natesuits <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/417979381332443136/d145fdbe6fea9d40b4a5e729859a2a2f.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_06-Feb-22 08:03 PM_:

Celeste can be used to challenge passed proposals within Conviction Voting and Tao voting by our community, so that mitigates some of the risk. If someone wishes to compete with the TEC on governance rights with the current parameters of our Bonding Curve (with the assumption that no Hatchers sell), they would need to put in ~15 million wxDAI. Considering we have a 22% entry tribute, a significant amount of those funds would go to the Common Pool (not a very logical attack). There is no way to challenge Snapshot voting, but these votes are also not binding, and can be evaluated and discussed within the community on their validity.

@JosephS

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/417979381332443136/d145fdbe6fea9d40b4a5e729859a2a2f.png](https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/417979381332443136/d145fdbe6fea9d40b4a5e729859a2a2f.png)

natesuits

_03-May-22 06:14 AM_:

Hi yall, probably all of you heard about Elon's takeover of Twitter. What do you think about it? Is it good or bad for the public? I must say that I am confused and unsure about the effect. And this is why I opened a discussion in Kialo (a super cool platform for collective sense making and discussions) about this question. Be happy if you'd join in! [https://www.kialo.com/is-elon-musks-takeover-of-twitter-good-for-the-public-58092?path=58092.0~58092.3](https://www.kialo.com/is-elon-musks-takeover-of-twitter-good-for-the-public-58092?path=58092.0~58092.3)

Is Elon Musk's takeover of twitter good for the public?

Does one person have the ability, to shape one of the most influential epistemic environments that became a public good, in a way that will benefit the general‚Ä¶

![https://www.kialo.com/images/24b244db-b633-4534-aa2a-2e44668deb5d_1200x630_stretched.jpeg](https://www.kialo.com/images/24b244db-b633-4534-aa2a-2e44668deb5d_1200x630_stretched.jpeg)

<h3>Mike Brunt <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/323858083996499969/a007514ed93a6cac73b4b767c74778aa.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_04-May-22 11:45 AM_:

I just wanted to share this with all of you; here in the South Willamette Valley in Oregon USA we have a major relocalization project underway called Incredible Edible Eugene. Part of this project is to build an Urban Permaculture Centre where all beds and systems are built from locall grown materials. These are composters and garden beds contructed from willow. Please reach out if you have any interest in doing something similar.

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/810744615048052767/971437402038091856/eugeneBackYardFarmer.jpg](https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/810744615048052767/971437402038091856/eugeneBackYardFarmer.jpg)

TE360 - Italy (Host: Davide, Italy)

From learning the first baby steps in Token Design & Engineering to discussing and sharing more advanced topics, TE360 Italy is a community and study group of like-minded individuals that value a structured approach to the design and testing of sustainable token ecosystems. Sessions are held primarily in Italian. If you want to learn more, click...
